 salmaan ke varisht vakil ashok mundargi kii taraf se pesh hue ek vakil pesh hue or unhone chuninda dastavej daayar karne ke liye kuch samay maanga or adaalat ne sunwaayee do hafte ke liye sthagit kar di

CBI will investigate the death of tigers in the Jim Corbettbaugh sanctuary
 uttarakhand ucch nyaayalay ne abhayaarany main pichley paanch saal main hui baaghon kii maut or unke shikaar main adhikariyon kii kathith sanliptata kii sibiai jaanch ke aadesh diye hai
 a division bench of Acting Chief Justice Rajiv Sharma and Justice Lokpal Singh on Tuesday ordered a CBI inquiry into the deaths of tigers in the last five years at Corbett Park
 adaalat ne sibiai ko baaghon ke shikaar main van adhikariyon kii sanliptata kaa pataa lagane ke bhi aadesh die
 The order states that the CBI will investigate the matter and its initial report will be presented to the court in sealed envelopes within three months
 sibiai jaanch main apni vanyajeev shakha kii sevaayen bhi le sakegi
 The court gave the order after it was made aware of the fact that only six of the nine tigers died in the park in the last six months were natural deaths
 adaalat ne kaha ki vah sibiai jaanch ke aadesh nahin detii lekin vartmaan maamla durlabh se durlabhtam shrenee kaa he jahaan sibiai kii visheshgyata kii prarthana kii gayi he
 The court also expressed concern that 40 tigers and 272 leopards have died in the state in the last two and a half years

 However, there were many more camps around, due to which the soldiers immediately started rescue work
 chalis javaanon ko surakshit nikaal liya gaya he
 Four are still missing while sixteen jawans could not be saved
 fouj ke javaanon ke liye ye barfbaari koi nai baat nahin
 Slipping of icy rocks is also not new to these troopers
 khilanmarg kii yah jagah bhi unke liye nayaa nahin
 But, the snow white havoc will break on them in this way, they never thought that because this area of khilanmarg is considered safe from Avalanch, that is the reason why the army chose this place for high altitude warfare training
 lekin, somvaar subah kareeb gyaarah baje barf kaa aisa tufaan uthaa ki kareeb 60 phogiyon kaa dal barf ke neeche aa gaya
 Army soldiers are trying to get their comrades out of the ice debris
 mausam ab bhi kharaab he or bachaav kaa kaam aasaani se nahin ho sakegaa
 In fact, every year the Army hosts High Altitude Warfare School here this season
 skool main sena ko khaastaur par oonchai vaale ilaakon main pahaado par chadhane, snow skiing or baaki chizon kii training di jaati he
 This time, five people, including about three and a half hundred trainee soldiers of the army, attended this training
 in logon ko 60-70 ke group main baanta gaya tha
 This is the reason that when the ice rocks slipped, only one team became its victim
 agar saare jawan ek hi jagah hote to nuksaan kahin zyada hota
 Not only this, but due to the presence of other soldiers, the work started immediately because there is a road jam due to snow up to 25 km from the spot
 aise main bachaav dal kaa pahunchnaa mushkil tha
 The Snow Avalanche Study Stabilization (SASE), which studied snow-slipping, had issued a warning on Sunday evening that there might be a rock-slipping event at high altitude, so people living at high altitude should move away from areas where the last three days It was snowing heavily
 kya hota he avalanchajab oonchi pahadiyon se badi maatra main barf kii chattaane girane lagati hai to wo avalanch kehalaata he
 Avalanche looks like an icy storm
 jab avalanch aata he to lagata he maano aasmaan se barf kaa pahaad tut rahaa ho
 It is so dangerous that even the strongest trees, rocks, whatever comes in its grip, it is difficult to escape
 agar avalanch khatarnaak ho to thode-se vakt main hi baari tabaahi much jaati he
 In mountainous areas where there is heavy snowfall, the risk of this is very high
 zyaadaatar avalanch mausam kii vajah se aate hai
 When the cold winds blow and the icy rocks do not stick to the slopes of the mountain, they start falling down
 kabhi-kabhi pahari par trekking ke dauraan bhi aise haadase ho jate hai
